< review>
I've been coming to this dental practice for over 35 years.  I began with Dr.  Lange when he was working in this same suite, and I worked for a company located in the same building. Now, at 76 years old, I am truly reaping the benefits. They have always been very professional, have the newest equipment, and the best dentists. Their fees may be on the high side, but you only have one set of teeth, and if you spend a little more to have everything done right, you will save your teeth and the costs associated with big problems down the road. I know, because my husband has always cut corners on his dental care. Now, he is looking at thousands of dollars for implants and various problems with teeth literally falling out from poor dental care from cut-rate dentists.

I have also been very satisfied with all the employees I've met over the years. Linda, at the front counter, has worked there for many years, and is a steady, professional fixture in their office. And Abbey, my personal hygienist, does a great job.  I am so comfortable while getting my teeth cleaned, I feel like I have come for a spa treatment.  Be good to yourself and make use of this beautiful dental practice.<//review>

<Review>For a first timer, it's fairly confusing - as recycling centers typically are. Small parking lot often overloaded, which if it backs up, leaves absolutely no way to queue in an organized way. Lot has only one combined entrance/exit which gets clogged by disorganized queueing.

Once you find a spot, you get out and look around for signs explaining what to do... See a long line of blue barrels... That's it? Look around for a blue barrel that hopefully someone hasn't laid claim to (there's a stash of "new" blue barrels but it's not clearly marked and often obscured by cars), then dump your stuff in there and... block the driveway while standing in a line, confused as the only visible sign is "express lane - 5 or less", but it appears closed (but even its closed-ness isn't clearly shown).

Recycling is one of those things I would have expected to be better over the years, not to have reached an all-time low for bad experience in 2020. CRV is long overdue for a revamp. Should be handled by machines. Today is the worst experience I ever had with recycling (after first visiting another center 5 miles away where I couldn't even stop the car, as there was no place to queue nor park).

The place is nice, clean, and runs quickly. The cashier doesn't try talking to you over the sound of crashing cans and bottles. That's nice. The process was quite quick once I managed to get to the front of the line with my one half-full barrel of crushed cans. And for my hour-and-a-half of driving and hassle, I came away $12.50 richer :)<//Review><Time>1593722391218<//Time></record></dataset><record>

Truly disappointing, I would give it no stars if I had a chance. My family and I just moved and were in search of a dog. We found a beautiful younger wired haired terrier in need of a home and immediately jumped on. After contacting Paws we were told that the dog was still available and we can come check him out. Today my parents went to go look at him in the morning. HE WAS THE BEST!!! We immediately fell in love with him more than we loved him in pictures. He was very energetic and super smart. We were told that the dog would be ours and the other applications would be thrown away. This evening we get an email that the dog needs to put under behavioral training and they were no longer interested in looking for a new home for him. We knew he needed training because his is still a young dog. We even said we would pay for professional training but they said no. <GmapID>0x80d9534c0bcd9a0f:0xc75828bda51732fc<//GmapID><username>Zen Wells< /username><Pictures>None</Pictures><response>None< /response><date>1474232400856</date>< Review>
This is one of the best organized and run Animal Care Facility in the country and should be an example for all shelters. The dogs each have separate rooms, NOT Cages, with windows for fresh air and a view!   They have daily outdoor playtime in the fenced play yards and are walked at least twice a day.  They are socialized so well that, when they are considered by a family to adopt, they are happy and well behaved and present beautifully. I know many people who have adopted from PAWS of Coronado and are very pleased with their new family members. The cats have large rooms, again no cages, with ladders and towers for climbing,  and lots of toys.  They are handled many times a day by a wonderful group of volunteers who socialize them and get them ready to fit right into their new adoptive homes. They are driven around the Landing in baby Prams so that they are available to be seen by potential adopters.   If you are looking for a great new family member to adopt, call for KAREN DWINELL, the outstanding adoption coordinator.  Pets bring so much joy into our lives and rescued ones bring even more!!< /Review>

<GmapID>0x80db7f2d26df191d:0x2077a29132aec605< /GmapID><Text>Briar Rose winery was magic üåü

For Labor Day weekend, I wanted to get away somewhere I hadn‚Äôt been before, but was in a short driving distance. I did some googling and found Snow White‚Äôs cottage. I am a HUGE original Disney fan (things from Walt‚Äôs time), so I knew I had to visit.

When we arrived, even the parking lot had a view. You had a gorgeous view of all the vineyards below you, and Briar Rose itself was covered from the outside with this whimsical type of bush. You enter the bush and all of a sudden, you find yourself in Snow White‚Äôs garden, surrounded by her cute squirrel friends, wishing well, and her seven dwarves.

The original quaint cottage was built in the 1970‚Äôs by Disney imagineer Beldon Fields. While working for Disney, Beldon collected bits and pieces of Disney artifacts which made their way into the cottage. Some tiles from Mr. Toads, a rock from Indiana Jones, and a lantern from Haunted Mansion make the grounds so much more special.

Beauty aside, the wine tasting is delicious. We started out with a wonderful cracker and homemade cheese kit while we waited on our wine. We got one red wine tasting, and one white wine tasting before ordering a couple extra glasses to enjoy the scenery a bit longer.

I cannot recommend Briar Rose enough! Delicious wine, knowledgeable staff, and a view to die for. I‚Äôll be coming back to Temecula just to enjoy the winery. üç∑

Want more reviews? Find me on Instagram @Dining_With_Davi<//Text><Rating>5<//Rating></record></dataset><record>

<user>117058046903318241770</user>< username>
L S<//username>
< Date>
1431266995997</Date>
<rating>4</rating>< review>
Our server was Eric. Learned few things while tasting their wines. Why red wine is red? Because of the processing technique: the grape skin is added while the wines is fermenting. That's what gives it a red color. This is also why the red wines have more beneficial properties. Unlike white wines that are processed without grape skin.
Why storing red wine bottles horizontally ? The red wine bottles should be laid flat so that sediment from the wine settles evenly on one side and the cork is submerged to the wine which keeps it moist. Dry corks will make your wine bitter.
Very interesting. It was my first ever experience with wine tasting. The place is quiet and green with roses and old house. I like that seats are outdoor under the trees shade. The only thing was not so pleasant is experience with hostess. Not friendly at all.< /review>

<UserId.>106660689015618577627<//UserId.><Review>Purchased the Groupon, but our server, Brandon, was super cool, giving us double shot tastings. The venue is super cutesie having the same name as Disney's Snow White, "Briar Rose".

If you look hard enough you may find all 7 of the dwarves hiding around the premises. Like Easter Eggs.

It's a small and intimate venue, a great setting for a party of 4-6, but romantic enough for two. The outdoor seating was in beautiful gardens with a variety of sculptures.

We purchased the "Talking Frog" for my cousin and ended up finishing 2 bottles. An interesting wine with some Hefeweizen, flavoring it like a beer.</Review><user_name>Jaznotes1<//user_name>< pictures>

<pictures>None<//pictures><Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
In 2011, I was a veteran dog owner, but a real dog training novice when I decided to train my elderly pit bull at Cali K9's occasional weekend classes in the Oakland Hills and Fremont. I quickly discovered there's a lot more to it than the standard "sit, stay, down" drill. Jas and his team trained me, not just my dog. And I also earned from watching other dog owners interact with their dogs in such a balanced way.

It was up to me to practice the training techniques I learned and use them consistently. This experience changed what became my last weeks with my 15-year-old best friend. Sadly, she was slowly dying of cancer and I eventually had to put her down. Around that time, I was home alone and was caught up in a scary armed home invasion robbery, which cemented my decision to re-evaluate and beef up my home security and get another canine companion.

A client of California K9 Solutions knew about a young Doberman rescue dog that needed a forever home. He was big, beautiful and friendly, but completely untrained and "all over the place". At the time, it was impossible for me to walk him down the street. Cali K9 trained me and my 95 lb. wild teenager at their facility in San Jose so I could take him anywhere. The 15 minutes of practice once or twice a day paid off and now I'm able to walk him off leash and feel confident he'll listen to me. In addition, he's turned into an amazing security dog, so I feel totally safe in my home and neighborhood. This whole experience turned into one of the best things that's ever happened to me. From the bottom of my heart, thank you Jas and company!< /review>

Pismo Beach didn't disappoint me. Actually, it never has. I'm the happiest when I'm near the ocean. Surprisingly there's lots of shops and outside dining available. The pier has been refurbished and fishing is once again allowed. Masks are required on the pier although only about half of the people were wearing them. It was a nice warm sunny day. If you've never been or haven't been in a while you owe yourself a visit.< /review>

< review>
Pismo Beach is a wonderful Mediterranean weathered place to visit! There are many hidden beaches that one may enjoy with few if any other people around. There are a variety of wineries to also visit along with some waterfalls that you can swim at and Lake Lopez where you can camp and wakeboard. Kayaking is also very beautiful with some caves that you can go through at Shell Beach. Don't miss the many miles of sand dunes that you can wander through south of Oceano. It is a wonderful place to see a beautiful sunset dropping into the blue jeweled Waters. Having lived here for 30 years I have been fortunate enough to experience all of the area's Many Wonders and would be happy to help others to find some of these secret places! Have you ever heard of the Dunites? They were an incredible people living in the Dunes that had a tremendous effect on the twentieth century yet no one knows about them anymore. Find out more on Instagram: @the_dunites_Utopia.</review>

< review>
I love Pismo Beach, and I've been coming here since before I could walk. Now with stores, restraunts, and parking being open the feel is like an escape to pre-COVID times. They're currently renovating the whole area surrounding the pier (new bathrooms, a park, slides down to the beach, tables, cornhole, etc.) And their new additions look amazing. They finally reopened parking near Wooly's at the end of Pomeroy which really helps with the flow of traffic. The beach is always clean, and it's a great place to hang out with friends, family, pets, or just go for a peaceful walk on your own. The one drawback is the sheer amount of people who smoke marijuana while walking down the street or on the beach; you literally can not escape the smell if you're anywhere near large groups of people. Otherwise it's great, and I'll definitely be back soon.< /review>

< review>
Alder said once it is completed, the hotel will feature a restaurant, pool and event lawn with fire pits and other amenities.

"It's very much a Central Coast beach cottage style," he said. "We didn't look to import Los Angeles to Pismo Beach. Obviously, we like Pismo Beach a lot. It should be a really nice getaway from the hustle and bustle of the major cities -- or the heat of the Central Valley, if that's what you're concerned about."

The hotel is expected to open in April or May 2019, Alder said.

"It's taken us a while to get going, but we're really excited," he said. "It's going to be very high-quality."<//review>
